**Query**

#### 获取用户详细画像信息

> 创建人: shangyuh

> 更新人: shangyuh

> 创建时间: 2025-05-09 10:16:02

> 更新时间: 2025-05-09 14:44:14

```text
暂无描述
```

**接口状态**

> 已完成

**接口URL**

> /open/private_marketing/user/detail

**请求方式**

> POST

**Content-Type**

> json

**请求Body参数**

```javascript
{
    "mobile": "15680795656",
    "info_key": "base"
}
```

| 参数名 | 示例值 | 参数类型 | 是否必填 | 参数描述 |
| --- | --- | ---- | ---- | ---- |
| mobile | 18280239732 | number | 是 | 完整手机号 |
| info_key | base | string | 是 | 要获取的具体画像的key base=基础画像信息(传base带画像标签，不传base不带画像标签) member=会员画像信息 consume=消费画像信息 action=行为画像信息 recreation=娱乐画像信息 socialize=社交画像信息 |

**认证方式**

> 继承父级

**响应示例**

* base-基础画像信息(200)

```javascript
{
	"code": 200,
	"sub_code": 0,
	"msg": "",
	"action": "",
	"data": {
		"base_info": {
			"profile_id": 13,
			"open_id": "o6IVz5SZxifS7ZREOAZCuAj7Pqks",
			"union_id": "oDsgf6cYv5KnPBGm-Um7unbOLTAI",
			"avatar": "https://zzyy.resource.i-ktv.com/biz/op/2025/04/08/uMc9amEo6KBMKPAAaqW8.jpeg",
			"wx_nickname": "段正军",
			"channel_name": "点餐",
			"follow_shop_names": [
				{
					"shop_id": 111,
					"shop_name": "音创演示厅",
					"follow_time": "2024-08-27 14:33:35",
					"del_type": 0
				},
				{
					"shop_id": 83,
					"shop_name": "李维的门店",
					"follow_time": "2024-09-24 15:35:59",
					"del_type": 0
				},
				{
					"shop_id": 182,
					"shop_name": "财升演示门店",
					"follow_time": "2025-04-10 16:19:51",
					"del_type": 0
				}
			],
			"member_id": "81",
			"labels": [
				{
					"name": "添加时间",
					"group_name": "组合或"
				}
			],
			"info_key": "base"
		},
		"member_info": {
			"info_key": "member"
		},
		"consume_info": {
			"info_key": "consume"
		},
		"action_info": {
			"info_key": "action"
		},
		"recreation_info": {
			"info_key": "recreation"
		},
		"socialize_info": {
			"info_key": "socialize"
		},
		"profile_id": 13
	}
}
```

| 参数名 | 示例值 | 参数类型 | 参数描述 |
| --- | --- | ---- | ---- |
| code | 200 | number | - |
| sub_code | 0 | number | - |
| msg | - | string | - |
| action | - | string | - |
| data | - | object | - |
| data.profile_id | 13 | number | 画像ID |
| data.base_info | - | object | 基础画像信息 |
| data.base_info.profile_id | 13 | string | 画像 |
| data.base_info.open_id | o6IVz5SZxifS7ZREOAZCuAj7Pqks | string | - |
| data.base_info.union_id | oDsgf6cYv5KnPBGm-Um7unbOLTAI | string | - |
| data.base_info.avatar | https://zzyy.resource.i-ktv.com/biz/op/2025/04/08/uMc9amEo6KBMKPAAaqW8.jpeg | string | 头像url |
| data.base_info.wx_nickname | 段正军 | string | 微信昵称 |
| data.base_info.channel_name | 点餐 | string | 客户来源名称 |
| data.base_info.follow_shop_names | - | array | 客户归属门店关系列表 |
| data.base_info.follow_shop_names.shop_id | 111 | number | 归属门店ID |
| data.base_info.follow_shop_names.shop_name | 音创演示厅 | string | 归属门店名称 |
| data.base_info.follow_shop_names.follow_time | 2024-08-27 14:33:35 | string | 添加时间 |
| data.base_info.follow_shop_names.del_type | 0 | number | 是否被客户删除 0=否,1=是 |
| data.base_info.member_id | 81 | string | 会员ID 大于0代表是注册会员,否则未注册会员 |
| data.base_info.labels | - | array | 画像标签详细列表 |
| data.base_info.labels.name | 添加时间 | string | 画像标签名称 |
| data.base_info.labels.group_name | 组合或 | string | 画像标签分组 |
| data.base_info.info_key | base | string | 画像的key |
| data.member_info | - | object | 会员画像信息 |
| data.member_info.info_key | member | string | 画像的key |
| data.consume_info | - | object | 消费画像信息 |
| data.consume_info.info_key | consume | string | 画像的key |
| data.action_info | - | object | 行为画像信息 |
| data.action_info.info_key | action | string | 画像的key |
| data.recreation_info | - | object | 娱乐画像信息 |
| data.recreation_info.info_key | recreation | string | 画像的key |
| data.socialize_info | - | object | 社交画像信息 |
| data.socialize_info.info_key | socialize | string | 画像的key |

* 无画像信息返回(200)

```javascript
{
	"code": 200,
	"sub_code": 0,
	"msg": "",
	"action": "",
	"data": {
		"profile_id": 0,
		"base_info": {},
		"member_info": {},
		"consume_info": {},
		"action_info": {},
		"recreation_info": {},
		"socialize_info": {}
	}
}
```

| 参数名 | 示例值 | 参数类型 | 参数描述 |
| --- | --- | ---- | ---- |
| code | 200 | number | - |
| sub_code | 0 | number | - |
| msg | - | string | - |
| action | - | string | - |
| data | - | object | - |
| data.profile_id | 0 | number | 画像ID |
| data.base_info | - | object | 基础画像信息 |
| data.member_info | - | object | 会员画像信息 |
| data.consume_info | - | object | 消费画像信息 |
| data.action_info | - | object | 行为画像信息 |
| data.recreation_info | - | object | 娱乐画像信息 |
| data.socialize_info | - | object | 社交画像信息 |
